The room is small, the window is even smaller, the curtains are not automatically controlled, the lighting design is extremely poor, the switch is inconvenient, and it is uncomfortable to work without a desk lamp. The table is big and small. It's okay for one person to eat, but it's very inconvenient for two people. You have to mop the table every time! The mini bar is super small, not to mention that you want to use a small coffee machine, there is none! The bagged coffee and tea are very low, and the free water is actually a bottle of ice dew for one yuan. The TV can't be on demand for movies and TV, only fixed programs can be watched. The toiletries in the bathroom are cheap and not easy to use. The toilet is not smart, and it is not a buffer cover! The toothbrush is not given a new one every day, and the paper towels are only available in the bathroom, and they are not in a whole pack. You have to go to the toilet to wipe your mouth after dining, and you have to prepare paper towels in advance in the middle of the night! Besides, the cleaning staff is not good enough, and they throw away the guests' autumn clothes. Their quality is low! I have stayed in many five-star hotels, but this one didn't have welcome snacks and fruits. You have to ask for fruits. The food delivery robot doesn't enter the room, so guests can only hold the door with one hand and take the food with the other hand. It's very difficult! The buffet breakfast has very few varieties, which can be said to be super few. It has the least variety in the five-star hotels I have experienced! I didn't want to go on the third day. In addition, I was refused to check out for two hours because I had to wait for the professor to finish the get out of class. But it was bad that there was no place to sit in the lobby. The few poor sofas were crowded with advertisers. We could only go to a nearby cafe to talk about things. In short, I won't come again. It's very bad. Don't waste your money on them!
